","AvailableDevicesNarratorText":"PC,Mobile","TypeTag":"app","RecommendationReason":"","LongDescription":"The Authlogics Authenticator turns your mobile device into a convenient, simple to use and highly secure Multi Factor Authentication token which can be used to log you into any system that uses Authlogics technology. This removes the need for users to carry things like key fobs, hardware tokens, card readers, USB devices or remember multiple PINs or passwords.\r\n\r\nImportant Note: The Authlogics Authenticator is an enterprise level solution, and therefore, for personal usage your device must be registered with a user account on an Authlogics Authentication Server before it can be used. This solution may be in use by a vendor that you utilise such as a bank or a city council. \r\n\r\nNOTE: If you are not affiliated to a vendor that utilises this resource, please do not install this Token as it will not serve a purpose for you.\r\n\r\n\r\nReplace PINs, Passwords and plastic key-ring tokens with the Authlogics Authenticator - the simple, memorable, secure authentication solution. This app contains two authentication types that are utilised as security tokens – PINgrid and PINpass.\r\n\r\n== PINgrid ==\r\n\r\nWhat if there was a password that was easy to remember, but it changed every time you used it?\r\n\r\nPINgrid is a revolutionary authentication technology that takes advantage of the mind’s hard-wired ability to remember patterns and shapes. It uses this handy human trait to provide a very robust, but brilliantly simple-to-use, logon system. PINgrid produces a one-time code (OTC) to prove who you are and all you have to remember is a simple pattern, no PINs or passwords. PINgrid keeps your pattern a secret by never revealing it when you log on. Each time you log in you enter a new code however your pattern remains the same and is secret to you.\r\n\r\nWhilst PINgrid can be used as a traditional 2 Factor Authentication solution it also suits many other scenarios. PINgrid 1.5 Factor Authentication allows for a secure One Time Code logon without having a secondary device at all which is well suited to easy access, medium security situations.
